[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The issue is reproducible through fuzzer-generated test cases, which typically [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Resource Allocation**: Examine code sections that:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocate memory based on input size[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Perform I/O operations or system calls in loops[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **State Machine Logic**: If applicable, review state machines or protocol [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m152[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mLOG.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipped XRef stream due to a corrupt offset:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, streamOffset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m153[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:                trailer = [0m[1;35mxrefTrailerResolver.getCurrentTrailer[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprev > [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfixedOffset > [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m && fixedOffset != prev[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:                throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"/Prev loop at offset "[0m[39m + prev[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Timeout Issue[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code analysis, the libFuzzer timeout is caused [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby multiple vulnerabilities in the Type1 font parser and PDF structure parsers. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese fall into three main categories:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Infinite loops due to missing null checks** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_3, vuln_4[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Uncontrolled memory allocation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_5, vuln_6[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Missing cycle detection in graph traversal** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_7, vuln_8[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Fix Infinite Loop in [0m[1;35mreadEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_3[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Problem:** The while loop continues indefinitely if the expected tokens [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"readonly"[0m[39m, or [0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are never found. When `[0m[1;35mpeekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns null, the loop [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcondition evaluates to true and continues forever.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fix:**[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a null check after calling `[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` inside the loop[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throw an IOException if null is encountered, indicating premature EOF[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature EOF: expected dup, readonly, or def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Infinite Loop in [0m[1;35mparseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_4[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.jav[0m[1;92ma:640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Problem:** Similar to vuln_3, the loop searching for [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[39m token [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinues indefinitely if the token is never found.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fix:**[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a null check after calling `[0m[1;35mnextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` inside the loop[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throw an IOException if null is encountered[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature EOF: expected CharStrings token"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Uncontrolled Memory Allocation in [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_5[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Lexer.jav[0m[1;92ma:502[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m515[0m[39m`[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Problem:** The method allocates `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlength[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` without validating the length [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter, which comes from untrusted input. Extremely large values cause OOM or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeout.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fix:**[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a maximum size constant at the class level[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validate the length parameter before allocation[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throw a DamagedFontException if length exceeds the limit[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add constant at class level [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m50[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final int MAX_CHAR_STRING_SIZE = 1_000_000;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Modify readCharString method:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate Token [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || length > MAX_CHAR_STRING_SIZE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharString length is invalid: "[0m[39m + length + [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m" [0m[32m([0m[32mmax: "[0m[39m + MAX_CHAR_STRING_SIZE + [0m[32m"[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mbuffer.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m space[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlength[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mbuffer.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return new [0m[1;35mToken[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, Token.CHARSTRING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBufferUnderflowException exception[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature end of buffer reached"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fix Integer Overflow in PfbParser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvuln_6[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:161[0m[39m`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Problem:** Integer overflow occurs when adding two int values before assigning to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlong, bypassing the MAX_LENGTH check.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fix:**[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35mreadSubrs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint lenIV[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m allocate size [0m[1;39m([0m[39marray indexes may not be in-order[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    int length = [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.INTEGER[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.intValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || length > MAX_SUBRS_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid subrs count: "[0m[39m + length + [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[32m" [0m[32m([0m[32mmax: "[0m[39m + MAX_SUBRS_COUNT + [0m[32m"[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < length; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mfont.subrs.add[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME, [0m[32m"array"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m rest of method[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Approach is Optimal[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: All fixes add defensive checks without changing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe core parsing logic, ensuring existing valid fonts continue to work.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Each fix is surgical and localized, reducing the risk of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Multiple layers of protection [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull checks, length [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation, cycle detection[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ensure robust handling of malformed inputs.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Standard Patterns**: Uses well-established patterns:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Set-based cycle detection for graph traversal[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input validation before resource allocation[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Proper null checking in loops[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Integer overflow prevention through type casting[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Informative Error Messages**: Each exception provides context about what went [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrong, aiding debugging.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Timeout Prevention**: All infinite loops are broken by either null checks or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcycle detection[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **DoS Mitigation**: Memory exhaustion attacks are prevented by size limits[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Integer Overflow**: Proper type casting prevents arithmetic overflow bypassing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity checks[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Maintains Compatibility**: Valid fonts/PDFs continue to parse correctly[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[3;91mFalse[0m[39m Positives on Limits**: Some legitimate [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut unusual[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fonts might exceed [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe limits[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Limits are set conservatively high [0m[1;39m([0m[39m1MB for charstrings, 10K [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor subrs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Can be adjusted based on real-world usage if needed[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance Impact**: Set operations add overhead to cycle detection[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Impact is negligible for normal files, only significant for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious inputs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich would timeout anyway[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Breaking Malformed-but-Parseable Files**: Some previously [0m[32m"working"[0m[39m corrupt [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfiles might now fail[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is intentional - these files are security risks and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould fail fast rather than hang[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already uses similar patterns:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;35mPDPageTree.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m304[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m314[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already has cycle detection using a Set[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple methods already validate for null tokens before processing[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The MAX_LENGTH constant pattern is already used in PfbParser[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy extends these existing best practices consistently across all [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerable code paths.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue is a libFuzzer timeout error. This type of error typically occurs[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The code enters an infinite loop or a very long-running loop[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Processing extremely large data structures[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Encountering malformed inputs that trigger inefficient algorithmic behavior[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue provides minimal details but indicates that the timeout occurred during [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing operations, suggesting that certain malformed or malicious inputs can cause[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe PDF/font parsing code to hang.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch attempts to address the timeout issue through several modifications:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Type1Parser.java modifications:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added `MAX_SUBRS_COUNT = 10_000` constant to limit the number of subroutines[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added null checks in two locations where `[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called in loops, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrowing `IOException` with descriptive messages if premature EOF is encountered[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Added validation in `[0m[1;35mreadSubrs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method to check if the subroutine count exceeds[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe maximum limit or is negative[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Type1Lexer.java modifications:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis within acceptable bounds[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. PfbParser.java modifications:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Understanding the Compilation Errors[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch attempted to fix a libFuzzer timeout by adding defensive checks and cycle[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetection mechanisms. However, it introduced two compilation errors in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XrefParser.java`:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Missing import for `Set` interface** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m102[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The patch uses `Set<Long> [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevSet = new HashSet<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` but didn't add the required import statement.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Reference to removed variable `lastPrev`** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m188[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The patch replaced [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lastPrev` variable with `prevSet` but didn't update all references to it.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Issues to Address[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report and code analysis reveal several timeout vulnerabilities:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m XrefParser.java - Inadequate cycle detection:**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Original code uses simple `lastPrev` comparison that only catches immediate loops[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Needs robust Set-based cycle detection to catch complex circular references[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Type1Parser.java - Unbounded loops:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Three unbounded while loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m563[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that call [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without null checks[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop at lines [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[39m searches for [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[39m token[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop at lines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m searches for [0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[39m, or [0m[32m"def"[0m[39m tokens  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Loop at lines [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m563[0m[39m searches for [0m[32m"Private"[0m[39m token[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Type1Parser.java - Unvalidated array allocation:**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mreadSubrs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m709[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m reads integer length without bounds checking[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Could allocate massive arrays causing memory exhaustion or extremely long loops[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Type1Lexer.java - Unvalidated buffer allocation:**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m502[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m accepts arbitrary length parameter[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Could allocate huge byte arrays causing memory exhaustion[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m PDPageTree.java - Missing cycle detection:**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- PageIterator constructor has recursive loop without cycle detection[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Could loop infinitely if page tree has circular references[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m PfbParser.java - Integer overflow:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Size calculation uses int arithmetic before converting to long[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Could overflow with malicious input[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI'll reapply the patches from the initial codebase with corrections for the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix XrefParser.java compilation errors[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add missing `import java.util.Set;` after line [0m[1;36m24[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replace all `lastPrev` logic with Set-based cycle detection[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove the redundant check at line [0m[1;36m173[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m176[0m[39m since cycle detection happens at loop [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add defensive limits to Type1Parser.java  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add `MAX_SUBRS_COUNT = 10_000` constant after line [0m[1;36m45[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add validation in `[0m[1;35mreadSubrs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before line [0m[1;36m710[0m[39m to check if length is negative or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceeds MAX_SUBRS_COUNT[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add null checks after `[0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls in three unbounded loops:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - After line [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m in the loop searching for [0m[32m"dup"[0m[35m/[0m[32m"readonly"[0m[35m/[0m[32m"def"[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - After line [0m[1;36m562[0m[39m in the loop searching for [0m[32m"Private"[0m[39m  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - After line [0m[1;36m643[0m[39m in the loop searching for [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add defensive limit to Type1Lexer.java[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add `MAX_CHAR_STRING_SIZE = 1_000_000` constant after line [0m[1;36m50[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add validation in `[0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` after line [0m[1;36m503[0m[39m to check if length is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegative or exceeds MAX_CHAR_STRING_SIZE[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Fix integer overflow in PfbParser.java[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change line [0m[1;36m161[0m[39m to use explicit long casting: `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlong[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtotal + [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlong[0m[1;39m)[0m[39msize`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Add cycle detection to PDPageTree.java[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add `Set<COSDictionary> seen = new HashSet<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` field after line [0m[1;36m182[0m[39m in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPageIterator[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add cycle detection at start of `[0m[1;35menqueueKids[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method after line [0m[1;36m207[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change `Collections.EMPTY_LIST` to `[0m[1;35mCollections.emptyList[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m224[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Comprehensive coverage**: Addresses all timeout vulnerabilities identified in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe evaluation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal changes**: Only modifies code directly related to timeout issues[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Follows existing patterns**: Uses patterns already present in the codebase [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;35mreadProc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows proper null checking pattern[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Reasonable limits**: Constants are set to values that accommodate legitimate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse while preventing abuse[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves functionality**: All defensive checks throw descriptive IOExceptions[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat maintain error handling consistency[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing logic:**[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XrefParser**: Set-based cycle detection is more robust than simple comparison [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut maintains same loop structure[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type1Parser**: Null checks prevent infinite loops but don't change parsing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic for valid input[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type1Lexer**: Size validation rejects malicious input but doesn't affect [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate CharStrings[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **PDPageTree**: Cycle detection prevents infinite loops but doesn't change page [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal for valid trees[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **PfbParser**: Long casting prevents overflow but doesn't change arithmetic for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid sizes[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the issues:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Compilation errors**: Fixed by adding missing import and properly replacing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall lastPrev references[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Timeout errors**: Fixed by adding bounds checking, cycle detection, and null [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks that prevent infinite loops[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory exhaustion**: Fixed by limiting array/buffer sizes to reasonable [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximums[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Rejection of edge cases**: Large but legitimate fonts might be rejected[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigated by setting generous limits [0m[1;39m([0m[39m10K subroutines, 1MB CharStrings[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error messages**: New IOExceptions provide clear diagnostics for debugging[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Performance**: Set operations add minimal overhead compared to timeout [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevention benefits[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar solutions in codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. PfbParser already uses MAX_LENGTH constant with validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mType1Parser.readProc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows proper null checking pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m476[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m478[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. PDPageTree already uses Set for page tracking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m50[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, extending pattern for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcycle detection[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
